### 11. 超逼真冬季雪花飞舞肖像提示词

**Author**: [Heisenberg](https://x.com/rovvmut_)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超现实的年轻女性冬季肖像，她正对着镜头吹雪，重点关注微观细节，例如可见的皮肤毛孔、自然的睫毛簇、PBR 材质和特定的色彩分级（冷青色-青色电影色调）。

![超逼真冬季雪花飞舞肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421939815_y0vsb0_G7iX6rWagAApYnJ.jpg)

```
{
  "Objective": "Create an ultra-realistic winter portrait of a young woman blowing snow toward the camera, with enhanced natural skin detail integrated smoothly into the prompt.",

  "Subject_Details": {
    "Age_Range": "young woman",
    "Expression": "lips pursed in a blowing gesture; eyes softly closed",
    "Hair": "short grey hair",
    "Clothing": "thick winter coat, knit mittens",
    "Skin_Detail_Enhancements": [
      "visible pores",
      "micro-creases",
      "natural skin sheen",
      "subtle reddish cast",
      "soft dryness on lips",
      "natural eyelash clustering"
    ]
  },

  "Pose_Instructions": {
    "Head": {
      "Position": "slightly forward",
      "Angle": "10–15° forward tilt",
      "Chin": "down"
    },
    "Arms_and_Hands": {
      "Elbows": "bent",
      "Hands": "mittens cupped together holding snow",
      "Hand_Position": "raised at chest height, forward-facing"
    },
    "Torso": "facing the camera directly",
    "Shoulders": "relaxed"
  },

  "Action": "young woman blowing snowburst particles toward the camera",

  "Camera_Settings": {
    "Lens": "50mm",
    "Aperture": "f/1.8–2.2",
    "Perspective": "eye-level",
    "Depth_of_Field": "shallow DoF with strong foreground snow bokeh"
  },

  "Lighting": {
    "Type": "diffused overcast winter daylight",
    "Qualities": [
      "soft even illumination",
      "subtle cool bounce from snow",
      "no harsh shadows"
    ]
  },

  "Environment": {
    "Location": "snowy forest",
    "Background": "blurred tree trunks with cold atmospheric haze",
    "Atmospherics": [
      "active snowfall",
      "blown snowburst in foreground"
    ]
  },

  "Materials_and_Textures": {
    "Mittens": "knit",
    "Coat": "matte winter fabric",
    "Hair": "soft wavy texture",
    "Snow": "powdery particles with micro-sparkle"
  },

  "Color_Grade": {
    "Palette": "cool teal-cyan filmic tones",
```

```
A vintage lo-fi poster design featuring a dark, retro living room. The main focus is a glowing 90s CRT TV displaying a retro soccer video game. Overlaid in the center is large, prominent typography: the word "OLD" in a hollow outline font, stacked above the word "DAYS" in a thick, solid white retro font. Create a dark, moody, photorealistic portrait of a young man (early 20s, slim face, pale skin, soft sharp jawline, messy medium-length wavy dark hair partially covering forehead). He is seated on a simple wooden chair, body slightly turned sideways, head tilted downward, eyes cast toward his hands in a contemplative, melancholic expression. He wears a black high-neck turtleneck under a long black overcoat with soft matte fabric. Normal wavy hair.
```
```
Background is a rough, textured wall with subtle stains and uneven paint, desaturated green-gray tones. Lighting is extremely low-key, coming from a soft side source (left side), creating deep shadows that partially obscure facial features while still keeping them faintly visible. Composition is medium shot, slightly off center framing. Add heavy film grain, analog noise, subtle blur, and muted color grading.
Keep everything natural and realistic: no stylization, no extra elements, no modern sharpness. Extremely grainy.
Maintain consistent shadows, realistic proportions, and a raw cinematic atmosphere with imperfect texture and slight noise artifacts.
```

### 22. 黑白电影感摩托车肖像

### 24. nano-banana-pro 的超逼真电影级转换提示

**Author**: [John](https://x.com/john87445528)  **Date**: 2026-03-10  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个专门为 nano-banana-pro 设计的详细图像生成提示，旨在将现有参考图像（如 MJ 生成的图像）转换为超现实、真人电影般的剧照。它侧重于将每个元素——角色、场景、道具和环境——转化为细节丰富、物理真实、电影级别的照片，强调深景深、胶片颗粒、戏剧性照明以及特定的电影技术规格，例如柯达 Vision3 500T 胶片。

![nano-banana-pro 的超逼真电影级转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773210667545_t9mobp_HDBZls9aMAA6JD7.jpg)
![nano-banana-pro 的超逼真电影级转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773210667533_iixszz_HDBaWNgaMAEw01b.jpg)

```
核心要求： 将参考图中的所有元素——包括角色、场景、道具、环境——全部转化为超写实真人实景，如同实地拍摄的电影剧照。
角色转化： 严格保留原角色的发型、服装、表情、五官特征、肢体动作与整体气质，转换为真实演员形象。
场景转化：
• 将漫画/插画场景还原为真实可拍摄的物理空间
• 所有道具、家具、建筑必须是实物搭景或实景取景
• 材质质感真实：布料褶皱、木纹肌理、金属反光、墙面纹理
• 环境细节丰富：灰尘、磨损痕迹、生活化细节
• 空间透视与光影符合物理规律
摄影风格：电影级实景摄影
• 深景深构图，前景到背景全部清晰
• 胶片质感，柔和颗粒与丰富色彩层次
• 戏剧化光影对比：暖色钨丝工作灯 vs 冷色自然暮光
• 主体突出，同时保留环境叙事性
• 如同《银翼杀手》《布达佩斯大饭店》级别的场景美术与摄影
技术规格：
• 胶片：Kodak Vision3 500T（电影摄影标准）
• 适用场景：夜景、低光环境、室内钨丝灯照明
• 光圈：f/8–f/11（深景深，全画面清晰）
• 焦段：35mm–50mm（标准电影视角）
• 分辨率：4K cinema 或更高
• 色彩：温暖饱和的钨丝灯色温，暗部细节保留
• 灯光设计：三点布光或自然光结合，营造电影级光影层次
场景美术要求：
• 实景搭建或外景取景，杜绝CG合成感
• 道具陈设符合角色背景与时代设定
• 空间设计有纵深感与生活气息
• 墙面、地板、天花板等环境元素具有真实质感
• 背景人物（如有）也需真实演员，避免模糊处理
反向提示词（严格避免）：
• 模糊背景、浅景深、散景、失焦
• 卡通、动漫、插画风、手绘质感、CG渲染感
• 平面化构图、缺乏空间纵深
• 假布景、绿幕合成痕迹、数字背景
• 面部变形、比例失调、AI生成痕迹
• 低质量、数字噪点、像素化、过度锐化
• 过曝强光、塑料质感、过度数字后期
• 道具悬浮、物理不合理、材质贴图感
• 空洞背景、缺乏细节、环境单调
参考风格： 电影摄影大师级作品 - Roger Deakins、Emmanuel Lubezki、Hoyte van Hoytema 的实景拍摄美学。
```

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2026-02-08  **Language**: en

```
Pedro Pascal and Sydney Sweeney performing figure skating together at the Winter Olympics. They are on an Olympic ice rink inside a large arena, surrounded by blurred spectators and soft stadium lights in the background. Both are mid-motion on the ice, synchronized and dynamic, captured in a candid, unposed moment.

Pedro Pascal wears a fitted Olympic figure-skating costume suitable for competition, focused expression, visible breath in the cold air. Sydney Sweeney wears a refined, elegant skating outfit, confident and joyful expression, hair styled for performance but slightly loose from movement. Natural body proportions, realistic skin texture with visible pores, subtle redness from the cold, no smoothing or artificial glow.

The ice surface shows skate marks, reflections, and imperfections. Breath vapor, slight motion blur on limbs, and natural sweat/frost details add realism. Lighting is authentic indoor arena lighting, uneven and practical—no cinematic spotlights, no studio look.

Photography style:
iPhone photography realism, handheld shot, slight framing imperfections, natural exposure, realistic white balance, no HDR look, visible film grain and digital noise, compressed highlights, soft shadows, shallow depth of field from phone portrait mode.

Mood & Vibe:
Authentic, documentary, spontaneous Olympic moment, grounded and human, emotionally real.

Camera & Technical Cues:

iPhone camera look

1× lens (≈26mm equivalent)

Handheld, slight motion shake

Natural arena lighting only

Film grain, mild noise, no skin retouching

Aspect Ratio:
3:4 

Negative Prompt:
plastic skin, beauty filters, airbrushed faces, cinematic lighting, studio lights, dramatic spotlighting, CGI look, hyper-sharp skin, waxy texture, unreal ice reflections, fantasy costumes, overprocessed HDR, glamour photography
```

### 71. 3x3 编辑照片拼贴联系表肖像

**Author**: [Mr Leslie.AI](https://x.com/Leslieyu0)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，旨在生成一个 3x3 网格的编辑照片拼贴画，模仿电影胶片样片，其中 9 个画面都展示同一个角色。它详细说明了服装（超大号海军蓝衬衫、象牙色长裤）、环境（都市阁楼、混凝土墙）以及姿势、表情和相机光学（混合镜头、胶片颗粒、浅景深）的细微变化。

![3x3 编辑照片拼贴联系表肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468615868_8wd002_G-mpXYHbcAAGnmV.jpg)

```
[Layout & Format] 3x3 grid editorial photo collage, a contact sheet of 9 cinematic frames, consistent character identity, high-end magazine layout. [Subject Core] A single character wearing an oversized dark navy shirt and ivory trousers, barefoot, relaxed authenticity, raw skin texture, hyper-realistic facial features, loose messy hair. ### 82. 魅惑的韩式美妆美食肖像提示
```

![Spontaneous Twilight Rome Convertible Shot](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967715074_n9q3ah_G75uy9DbsAANiiR.jpg)

```
A raw, spontaneous iPhone photograph captured at twilight in {argument name="city" default="Rome"}, showing a young woman with windswept hair laughing as she leans out the window of a {argument name="car model" default="classic Alfa Romeo convertible"}. Warm city lights and the fading sunset catch the genuine joy on her face. The background is a motion-blurred wash of vespas, historic buildings, and pedestrians, emphasizing the car's movement while keeping her sharply in focus. **Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en
```

> 一个复杂的 JSON 提示，专为图像编辑设计，旨在将现有图像转换为高端时尚杂志肖像。它严格保留了拍摄对象的面部特征和原始姿势，同时更新了服装（亚麻衬衫、靛蓝色牛仔裤、运动鞋），并应用了特定的电影级照明和技术风格（浅景深、细微胶片颗粒、暖焦糖色调）。

```
{
  "type": "image_edit_prompt",

  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "notes": "Maintain the woman's exact facial structure, proportions, expression, and skin texture from the uploaded image."
  },
  "pose": {
    "keep_original_pose": true,
    "description": "Seated on the right arm of a mid-century brown leather sofa, leaning slightly forward, hands loosely clasped over the right knee, left foot flat on the floor, right ankle slightly raised."
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "crisp white open-collar linen shirt with sleeves rolled to mid-forearm",
    "bottoms": "slim straight indigo jeans cuffed at the ankle",
    "footwear": "clean white low-top leather sneakers",
    "accessories": [
      "minimal silver watch on the left wrist"
    ],
    "additional_elements": {
      "blazer": "lightweight navy blazer casually draped over the back of the sofa"
    }
  },
  "lighting_mood": {
    "key_light": "soft natural window light from camera-left",
    "background": "warm beige backdrop",
    "rim_light": "gentle rim light to create separation from background",
    "color_grade": "warm caramel / beige fashion editorial tone"
  },
  "technical_style": {
    "look": "high-end fashion, cinematic",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow (around f/2.8)",
    "lens_perspective": "50mm equivalence",
    "contrast": "medium",
    "grain": "subtle film grain",
    "retouching": "realistic skin retouch (retain pores and natural texture)",

      "sharpen eyes",
      "enhance fabric textures",
      "boost catchlights"
    ]
  },

  },

    "finish": "realistic, polished fashion editorial",

  },
```

### 102. 电影感怀旧快照生成器

**Author**: [GENEL | 動画生成AI](https://x.com/genel_ai)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的提示词，用于生成具有电影感、怀旧和情感氛围的日常快照。它指定了温暖的黄调光线、降低的对比度、细微的胶片颗粒，以及针对阴影（偏蓝）和高光（金色）的特定色彩分级。

```
シネマティックでノスタルジックな雰囲気のスナップ写真。
やわらかい光、少し黄味がかったあたたかい色味にして、全体のコントラストを少し下げてください。
フィルム写真のようなわずかなフィルムグレインを追加し、影はほんの少し青みがかったトーンにして、ハイライトは黄金色にしてください。
背景は少しボケたようにやわらかく、日本のローカルな風景のような、静かで懐かしい空気感を出してください。

▼動画化する場合
プロンプトに「The camera shakes.（カメラは手ブレ）」と入れると臨場感が出ます💡
```

### 104. 紧凑型数码相机屏幕快照：一位年轻女性

![紧凑型数码相机屏幕快照：一位年轻女性](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765106417906_0olqp2_G7SgEsUbEAA-WXL.jpg)

```
使用附件照片的面部特征。一台小巧的佳能数码相机屏幕上显示着年轻女子的特写镜头。相机机身环绕着图像，可见其按钮、拨盘和纹理表面，包括FUNC/SET转轮、DISP按钮以及侧面的“IMAGE STABILIZER”标签。屏幕上的照片拍摄于夜晚的室内，明亮的机内闪光灯照亮了女子的脸庞和头发，在她脸上和发丝间形成锐利的高光。她深色的长发松散地垂落在脸颊旁，双唇微张，表情柔和。闪光灯凸显了她的五官，背景是昏暗杂乱的厨房，隐约可见电器、架子和金属表面，呈现出柔和的虚化效果。整体氛围自然、真实、怀旧，让人想起2000年代初的数码相机快照。色调偏冷且略微柔和，闪光灯形成强烈对比，屏幕显示带有自然颗粒感。照片预览内无文字或标识。

比例：4:5竖版

相机：紧凑型数码相机模拟  
镜头：等效28–35mm  
光圈：f/2.8  
感光度：ISO 400  
快门速度：1/60秒（使用闪光灯）  
白平衡：自动闪光  
光线：主体受强烈直射闪光灯照明，背景为微弱环境光  
调色风格：怀旧数码相机色调、高对比闪光效果、细腻的屏幕颗粒感、真实的屏幕辉光。
```

**Author**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne)  **Date**: 2026-03-26  **Language**: en

> 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的结构化 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张 Sadie Sink 的 3 帧垂直拼贴画，采用闪光摄影。该提示词强调了跨帧的严格身份一致性、自然的皮肤纹理、特定的服装（黑色细肩带上衣），以及在卧室环境中营造出坦率、亲密的夜间美学。

```
        "top frame: resting face on one hand, lips slightly pursed",

      "setting": "bedroom",
      "background": "soft bed linens, pillows, bedside table with warm lamp light, slightly blurred depth"
```

```
  Morphology:   `Extreme wide-angle fisheye distortion, dynamic contorted mid-air pose, curved ramp geometry::3`
  Material Physics:   `Scuffed grip tape, splintered plywood, sticker-bombed surfaces, shiny metal trucks, worn canvas skate shoes::3`
```

**Author**: [AIArtChino](https://x.com/aiartchino)  **Date**: 2026-01-24  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张逼真的、抓拍的日本年轻女白领（OL）肖像。该提示旨在实现特定的美学效果：年轻的光泽、专业而朴素的服装（旨在弱化身材），以及诸如昏暗夜间办公室环境中的闪光摄影、胶片颗粒和柔焦等技术规格。

![日本办公室女郎 (OL) 的写实抓拍肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769322360770_y5pbti_G_dYnkJa8AAebyD.jpg)
![日本办公室女郎 (OL) 的写实抓拍肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769322360847_3yuzbi_G_dYnkHbYAArcHm.jpg)

```
visual_blueprint:
  full_prompt: |
    Create a highly aesthetic, photo-realistic candid portrait of a cute young Japanese office lady (OL) who appears to be in her early 20s. 
    She has a soft, youthful face with large expressive eyes, delicate fair skin that glows naturally, subtle natural makeup, and dark hair in a simple soft hairstyle—straight or gentle waves with neat bangs falling naturally. 
    Her expression is calm and professional, with a subtle polite smile and soft eyes that give an innocent yet composed vibe.
    She has a naturally voluptuous figure with large breasts, but in keeping clothing to downplay their chest—she wears a classic Japanese OL suit designed to subtly conceal and not emphasize her bust: a loose-fitting crisp white long-sleeve blouse (slightly oversized or with soft draping fabric that avoids tight tension across the chest), paired with a tailored {argument name="jacket color" default="navy or black"} jacket worn buttoned or semi-buttoned for added coverage, and a knee-length pencil skirt or straight slacks. 
    The overall fit is professional and modest, with gentle fabric drape and no visible cleavage or tight contours around the chest area.
    The shot is an upper-body portrait framed from the chest up, showing her standing casually yet professionally in a relaxed posture—shoulders soft, perhaps holding a folder or with hands lightly clasped in front for a natural office feel.
    The photo is captured using flash photography in a low-light, dim indoor office atmosphere at night, with slight overexposure from the flash creating a soft, flattering glow on her youthful skin. 
    Include realistic film grain and subtle color noise for a raw, authentic feel, soft focus overall with shallow depth of field, and a beautifully blurred nighttime office background with warm bokeh from desk lamps and subtle window glow showing city lights.
```

> 一个超写实编辑肖像的详细提示，采用原始闪光摄影，描绘一位年轻女性手持华丽的威尼斯假面舞会面具，背景是模糊的黑暗城市天际线。

![超写实主义编辑肖像，带原始闪光效果](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977303692_m58sbq_G_G2l4XW0AA26hb.jpg)
![超写实主义编辑肖像，带原始闪光效果](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977304106_pinfwp_G_G2l4VXkAAqZA1.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_configuration": {
    "type": "Ultra Photorealistic Editorial Portrait",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "style_model": "Raw Flash Photography"
  },
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject_description": {
      "identity": "Exceptionally beautiful young woman, early 20s, magnetic screen presence, effortless confidence.",
      "hair": "Long, thick dark brown hair with soft volume, slightly tousled, framing the face and falling forward over both shoulders.",
      "face": "Striking symmetrical face, large expressive eyes with intense eye contact, relaxed brows, soft glossy lips slightly parted, natural confident smile.",
      "pose": "Standing very close to the camera with a subtle forward lean from the waist. Shoulders gently rolled back and chest naturally lifted. Chin slightly lowered while eyes look straight into the lens for strong intimacy. Right hand raised near cheek level, clearly holding an ornate Venetian masquerade mask angled outward and fully visible. Left hand resting at the hip to accentuate curves."
    },
    "attire_and_accessories": {
      "outfit": "{argument name="dress color" default="green"} sequin dress with thin straps and a deep, elegant neckline that naturally frames cleavage without exaggeration. Fabric catches flash light with intense sparkle.",
      "accessories": [
        "Ornate silver-and-black Venetian masquerade mask with detailed filigree, held in the right hand.",
        "Minimal diamond necklace sitting just above the neckline."
      ]
    },
    "environment_and_atmosphere": {
      "setting": "Luxury rooftop or balcony at night.",
      "background": "Very dark, softly blurred city lights with no distractions.",
      "lighting": "Direct flash placed slightly above eye level, sculpting the eyes, cheekbones, collarbones, neckline, and mask"
```

### 132. Candid Direct-Flash 模拟条形快照

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张坦率、低保真、模拟胶片风格的照片，照片中有两名女性（一名金发女性穿着黑色紧身胸衣，一名深色头发女性穿着印花抹胸），她们亲密地坐在一间复古风格、光线昏暗的酒吧里。该提示强调了刺眼的直射机内闪光灯、厚重的胶片颗粒感以及俏皮、随意的互动。

### 140. 超逼真的智能手机夜间抓拍照片提示词

**Author**: [zayan](https://x.com/HustleXR)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张在东京夜晚拍摄的超逼真、抓拍式智能手机照片。该提示强调运动模糊、刺眼的闪光灯照明、噪点和不完美的构图，以实现原始、真实和未经雕琢的美感，同时严格要求使用参考图像来确定面部比例，但不复制人物身份。

![超逼真的智能手机夜间抓拍照片提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544778848_gokrhc_G-rof3LbMAAGR20.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic candid smartphone photograph, 9:16 vertical.
Use the attached image only as a strong visual inspiration for general facial proportions and vibe,
while ensuring the generated subject remains fully original, non-identifiable, and not a face copy.
Scene
Nighttime on a quiet Tokyo city sidewalk beside a building with white ceramic tile walls.
The subject is walking past the camera, partially side-on, captured mid-step in a rushed, accidental moment.
Poses & Gestures (combined naturally)
The subject reacts instinctively to being photographed:
turning her head back mid-walk as if surprised,
raising one hand close to the lens to partially block the camera,
shy, restrained smile forming as she suppresses laughter,
body angled in half-profile while continuing to walk forward,
motion carries her slightly out of frame, imperfect framing.
Expressions are subtle and spontaneous — embarrassed, playful, fleeting — never posed.
Camera & Motion
Shot on a modern smartphone, handheld, rushed capture. Strong uncontrolled camera shake. Heavy directional motion blur across the raised hand, hair, and face. Facial features appear smeared and streaked by movement, faintly recognizable but distorted. Partial ghosting around the body. Imperfect framing, subject nearly leaving the frame.
Lighting
Flash-only lighting fired mid-motion. Harsh flash highlights on skin and hand. Deep surrounding darkness. Uneven exposure, blown highlights, hard shadows typical of hurried night phone photography.
Background
White ceramic tile wall stretches into streaked light bands due to motion blur. Street surroundings fade into darkness with minimal readable detail.
Mood
Candid, shy, slightly playful. Feels intrusive, raw, imperfect, and authentic — like a fleeting memory accidentally captured and never meant to be perfect.
Image Quality
Extremely noisy. Heavily blurred. Raw smartphone look. Not cinematic. Not editorial. Not polished.
Negative Prompt
anime, illustration, painting, stylized,
studio lighting, beauty lighting, soft portrait,
sharp focus, clean face, perfect anatomy, smooth skin,
fashion editorial, posed portrait, cinematic grading, film still,
tripod shot, professional photography,
identity match, face copy, real person replication
```

> 一个用于生成 2000 年代初期数码相机闪光快照美学风格肖像的结构化提示。它详细描述了一位年轻女性，她有着乌黑的头发和霓虹紫色的挑染，身穿黑色紧身胸衣和 Y2K 配饰，强调了刺眼的机载闪光灯照明和抓拍的网红风格。

```
{
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, light skin tone",
      "hair": "Long, straight jet-black hair with neon purple chunky highlights framing the face, center part",
      "expression": "Confident pout with slightly raised eyebrows, direct eye contact with camera",
      "pose": "Standing front-facing, both hands lifting hair strands outward near collarbone"
    },

      "top": "Black strapless corset top with lace trim and visible boning, snug fit",
      "accessories": [
        "Sheer black mesh fingerless gloves",
        "Chrome heart-style choker necklace",
        "Low-slung silver chain belt at hips"
      ]
    },
    "makeup": {
      "eyes": "Bold winged eyeliner, voluminous lashes, sharp brows",
      "lips": "Glossy nude-pink lipstick"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Indoor hallway or gallery space",
      "background": "Large framed abstract artwork in deep blue and black tones"
    },

      "aesthetic": "Early-2000s digital camera, Y2K party-girl influencer style",
```

### 185. 超现实超逼真三文鱼柳世界提示

> 一个极具创意和超现实的提示，用于生成一个等距、超现实的场景：所有事物，包括河流，都由不同颜色的三文鱼柳构成，所有元素都拟人化，并以强烈的闪光摄影捕捉。

![超现实超逼真三文鱼柳世界提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765990893245_mln6p1_G7-D9nXXcAcX0gi.jpg)

```
Let’s make it NYC 

Salmon in the river, but it's salmon fillets

but the river is also fillets

this world is a universe of diff coloured fillets (ie the river = blue fillets) …. hyperrealistic harsh flash

isometric

zoom out i want to see the whole scenery 

it needs to feel like a real living world

everything is anthropomorphic
```

```

    ],
```

### 187. 复古美学胶片摄影提示

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: en

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 生成一张年轻女性全身复古风格照片的详细提示。图片中包含特定的服装（红色连体衣、白色及膝袜、红色运动鞋）、独特的妆容（泛红的粉色脸颊）、道具（复古相机）以及直射闪光灯照明和颗粒感胶片美学等技术细节。

![复古美学胶片摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765990996683_eeoz46_G78pZk4agAA7T24.jpg)

```
A vibrant, full-body shot, captured in a soft, vintage-style photograph, features a young woman with long, dark, wavy hair sitting casually on a wooden chair with metal legs. She wears a white t-shirt with a red graphic print layered under a full-length red jumpsuit with long sleeves, covering her from neck to toe. She still wears white knee-high lace socks with frilly tops and red sneakers with white logos for added retro charm. Her left leg is bent, with her foot resting on the chair, while her right leg extends forward.

Her makeup is distinctive, with heavily flushed pink cheeks and nose, winged eyeliner, and glossy lips. Small red bows sit in her hair, and her fingernails are painted blue. In her left hand, she holds a vintage green and black point-and-shoot camera resting on her knee. Her right hand is raised, with her fingers touching her temple, giving a thoughtful or relaxed pose.

The background includes a light yellow wall and a window with a sheer white curtain. To her right, a vintage-style “Canister” jar sits on the windowsill. A plant is visible in the lower left corner. The lighting resembles a direct flash, creating bright, slightly harsh illumination on the subject, highlighting her skin and clothing textures while casting sharp shadows. The warm, saturated color grading gives the image a playful, retro, dreamy aesthetic reminiscent of grainy film photography.

Use photo reference for facial features.
```

[[Flash Photography]] [[Film Grain]] [[Retro Fashion]]

### 188. 2000 年代初期数码相机闪光灯肖像提示词

**Author**: [Harboris](https://x.com/Harboris_27)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细图像生成提示，旨在重现一张坦率、怀旧的年轻男子肖像，该肖像显示在一台紧凑型佳能数码相机的屏幕上，强调刺眼的直射闪光灯照明、柔和的色彩和真实的屏幕光晕，让人联想到 2000 年代初期的数码摄影。

![2000 年代初期数码相机闪光灯肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765990991603_tdjoe8_G779O2jagAQLkpF.jpg)

```
Use the facial features of the attached photo. A close-up shot of a young man displayed on the screen of a compact Canon digital camera. The camera body surrounds the image with its buttons, dials, and textured surface visible, including the FUNC/SET wheel, DISP button, and the “IMAGE STABILIZER” label along the side.

The photo on the screen shows the young man indoors at night, illuminated by a bright built-in flash that creates sharp highlights on his face and hair. He has short, slightly messy dark hair with loose strands framing part of his forehead, and a soft, slightly open-lip expression.

The flash accentuates his features against a dim, cluttered kitchen background with appliances, shelves, and metallic surfaces softly blurred. The mood is candid, raw, nostalgic, and reminiscent of early 2000s digital camera snapshots. Colors are slightly muted with cool undertones, strong flash contrast, and natural grain from the display. No text, no logos inside the photo preview itself.

Scale ratio: 4:5 vertical
Camera: compact digital camera simulation
Lens: equivalent to 28–35mm
Aperture: f/2.8
ISO: 400
Shutter speed: 1/60 with flash
White balance: auto flash
Lighting: harsh direct flash on subject, ambient low light in the background
Color grading: nostalgic digital camera tones, high contrast flash, subtle display grain, authentic screen glow.
```

```
      }

      "location": "Subway / Underground train station platform",
```

### 193. Y2K 圣诞咖啡馆闪光肖像提示

**Author**: [毎日の活力⚡](https://x.com/_dailyboost)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张 Y2K 数码相机风格的超写实女性肖像，特点是闪亮的黑色皮夹克、抖音/韩式妆容、咖啡馆背景中的圣诞装饰，以及用于打造高对比度、明亮肤色效果的刺眼直射闪光灯。

![Y2K 圣诞咖啡馆闪光肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440027565_t6sfr2_G7ubIHabEAAQrmE.jpg)

```
Create a hyper-realistic portrait of a cute woman using my reference image. She is sitting with her chin resting on her hand at a dark wooden table in front of a vintage-style café.

Fashion & Outfit:
She wears a shiny black leather jacket, slightly open to reveal a white inner top, showing a beautiful neckline. Matched with a fitted black mini-skirt set. She also wears black fishnet stockings. Add a fluffy fur hat over her outfit.

Background:
In front of a marble-grey café exterior, decorated with a Christmas theme. Include a realistic Christmas tree, pine decorations, and festive ornaments.

Lighting & Tone:
Warm orange tungsten lighting for an inviting, cozy atmosphere, combined with a strong direct flash hitting the subject straight on, making her skin bright and glowing, contrasting with the slightly darker background.
The photo should feel Y2K digital compact-camera style—sharp 8K resolution, realistic skin texture, with light film grain.

Hair & Makeup:
Long dark-brown hair blowing slightly in the wind, messy layered strands with a few pieces softly covering part of her face—stylish, cool, and subtly sexy.
Her skin is very fair.
Makeup style: Douyin/Korean—long curled lashes, soft flushed pink blush on cheeks and nose tip, glossy pink lips.
She has Christmas-themed nail art.

Props:
On the table:
• A large bouquet wrapped in brown kraft paper, containing cotton flowers and pine leaves.
• A gold Canon IXY 30S camera placed on the table.

She holds a Christmas-decorated drink in her right hand and smiles slightly.

Additional Visual Style:
The flash creates extremely bright, slightly yellow-tinted skin with a hard shadow behind her.
High-contrast, ultra-sharp 8K image.
Warm ambient sunlight.
Fuji Film Pro 400H color style with old-lens filter and light film grain.
The subject should appear bright and stand out clearly from the background.
```

[[Flash Photography]] [[Y2K Aesthetic]] [[Fashion Portrait]] [[Christmas Theme]]

### 194. 超逼真 Y2K 数码相机风格肖像

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的图像生成提示，用于创作一张超现实、高对比度的可爱亚洲女性肖像，置身于一个节日气氛浓厚的圣诞主题咖啡馆中。利用强闪光灯和暖钨丝灯光，营造出 Y2K 数码傻瓜相机的美学效果，画面中人物皮肤发光，并带有胶片颗粒感。

![超逼真 Y2K 数码相机风格肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440030612_gdiaj0_G7uWyXeWIAI1E7E.jpg)

```
Create a hyper-realistic portrait of a cute Asian woman. She is sitting with her chin resting on her hand at a dark wooden table in front of a vintage-style café.

Fashion & Outfit:
She wears a shiny black leather jacket, slightly open to reveal a white inner top, showing a beautiful neckline. Matched with a fitted black mini-skirt set. She also wears black fishnet stockings. Add a fluffy fur hat over her outfit.

Background:
In front of a marble-grey café exterior, decorated with a Christmas theme. Include a realistic Christmas tree, pine decorations, and festive ornaments.

Lighting & Tone:
Warm orange tungsten lighting for an inviting, cozy atmosphere, combined with a strong direct flash hitting the subject straight on, making her skin bright and glowing, contrasting with the slightly darker background.
The photo should feel Y2K digital compact-camera style—sharp 8K resolution, realistic skin texture, with light film grain.

Hair & Makeup:
Long dark-brown hair blowing slightly in the wind, messy layered strands with a few pieces softly covering part of her face—stylish, cool, and subtly sexy.
Her skin is very fair.
Makeup style: Douyin/Korean—long curled lashes, soft flushed pink blush on cheeks and nose tip, glossy pink lips.
She has Christmas-themed nail art.

Props:
On the table:
• A large bouquet wrapped in brown kraft paper, containing cotton flowers and pine leaves.
• A gold Canon IXY 30S camera placed on the table.

She holds a Christmas-decorated drink in her right hand and smiles slightly.

Additional Visual Style:
The flash creates extremely bright, slightly yellow-tinted skin with a hard shadow behind her.
High-contrast, ultra-sharp 8K image.
Warm ambient sunlight.
Fuji Film Pro 400H color style with old-lens filter and light film grain.
The subject should appear bright and stand out clearly from the background.
```

### 195. 2000 年代数码相机快照提示

```
{
  "subject": {
    "type": "Young woman",
    "appearance": {
      "hair": "Golden blonde, long layered cut with curtain bangs, textured beach waves, slightly messy 'bedhead' volume",

      "eyes": "Hazel-green, looking over sunglasses frame, seductive squint",

    }
  },
  "fashion": {
    "apparel": {
      "item": "Sequin tube top or dress",
      "color": "{argument name="sequin color" default="Champagne gold / Silver mix"}",
      "texture": "High-reflectivity sequins creating distinct glitter/sparkle points"
    },
    "accessories": {
      "eyewear": "90s style rectangle rimless sunglasses, brown gradient lenses, gold bridge, positioned low on nose",
      "jewelry": [
        "Stacked chunky gold dome rings on multiple fingers",
        "Cartier-style gold love bangles on wrist"
      ]
    }
  },
  "pose": {
    "type": "Car selfie / Candid close-up",
    "angle": "Slight high angle, tilted frame (Dutch angle)",
    "gesture": "Right hand adjusting sunglasses frame, left hand splayed on chest showcasing jewelry"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Luxury car interior (black leather visible)",
    "lighting_context": "Nighttime city driving",
    "background_details": "Out-of-focus city lights (bokeh) through rear window, dark moody cabin atmosphere"
  },
  "technical_parameters": {
    "lighting_style": "Hard direct flash (on-camera), high contrast, minimal diffusion",
    "color_grading": "Warm golden tones, saturated skin tones, deep blacks in shadows",
    "camera_simulation": {
      "camera_type": "High-end compact digital (e.g., Canon G7X Mark II) or iPhone 15 Pro with Flash",

      "aperture": "f/2.8 (sharp subject, creamy bokeh background)",

      "shutter": "Fast shutter to freeze flash action"

}
```

```
{
  "style": "hyper-realistic iPhone flash selfie, late-night bedroom vibe",
  "age_range": "21–24 years old",
  "girl": {
    "hair": "jet-black straight hair with blunt bangs, shoulder-blade length, perfectly sleek and shiny",
    "face": "pale skin, sharp winged eyeliner, overdrawn matte nude lips, slight resting bitch face",
    "eyes": "fox-like upturned eyes, heavy lower lash line, staring straight into lens with zero emotion",

  },

    "fit": "baggy on top, contrast against tiny waist"
  },

    "lighting": "room almost completely dark except aggressive red LED strips behind posters + cold white phone flash"

    "heavy jewelry",

    "smooth plastic skin"
```
